= Date of the <i>Villa</i> and <i>Ciudad</i> charters</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Ponce</b> (<span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1177148991">.mw-parser-output .IPA-label-small{font-size:85%}.mw-parser-output .references .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .infobox .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .navbox .IPA-label-small{font-size:100%}</style><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small"><a href="/wiki/American_English" title="American English">US</a>: </span><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt" lang="en-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\xcb\x88</span><span title="&#39;p&#39; in &#39;pie&#39;">p</span><span title="/\xc9\x94\xcb\x90/: &#39;au&#39; in &#39;fraud&#39;">\xc9\x94\xcb\x90</span><span title="&#39;n&#39; in &#39;nigh&#39;">n</span><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span><span title="/e\xc9\xaa/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;face&#39;">e\xc9\xaa</span></span>,<span class="wrap"> </span><span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\xcb\x88</span><span title="&#39;p&#39; in &#39;pie&#39;">p</span><span title="/o\xca\x8a/: &#39;o&#39; in &#39;code&#39;">o\xca\x8a</span><span title="&#39;n&#39; in &#39;nigh&#39;">n</span></span>-/</a></span></span> <a href="/wiki/Help:Pronunciation_respelling_key" title="Help:Pronunciation respelling key"><i title="English pronunciation respelling"><span style="font-size:90%">PAWN</span>-say, <span style="font-size:90%">POHN</span>-</i></a>, <span class="rt-commentedText nowrap"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1177148991"><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small"><a href="/wiki/British_English" title="British English">UK</a>: </span><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt" lang="en-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\xcb\x88</span><span title="&#39;p&#39; in &#39;pie&#39;">p</span><span title="/\xc9\x92/: &#39;o&#39; in &#39;body&#39;">\xc9\x92</span><span title="&#39;n&#39; in &#39;nigh&#39;">n</span></span>-/</a></span></span> <a href="/wiki/Help:Pronunciation_respelling_key" title="Help:Pronunciation respelling key"><i title="English pronunciation respelling"><span style="font-size:90%">PON</span>-</i></a>, <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1177148991"><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small">Spanish:</span> <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="es-419-Latn-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">&#91;\xcb\x88ponse&#93;</a></span> <span class="noprint"><span class="ext-phonos"><span data-nosnippet="" id="ooui-php-1" class="ext-phonos-PhonosButton noexcerpt ext-phonos-PhonosButton-emptylabel oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-buttonElement oo-ui-buttonElement-frameless oo-ui-iconElement oo-ui-buttonWidget" data-ooui="{&quot;_&quot;:&quot;mw.Phonos.PhonosButton&quot;,&quot;href&quot;:&quot;\\/\\/upload.wikimedia.org\\/wikipedia\\/en\\/transcoded\\/f\\/fb\\/Ponce2.ogg\\/Ponce2.ogg.mp3&quot;,&quot;rel&quot;:[&quot;nofollow&quot;],&quot;framed&quot;:false,&quot;icon&quot;:&quot;volumeUp&quot;,&quot;data&quot;:{&quot;ipa&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;text&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;lang&quot;:&quot;en&quot;,&quot;wikibase&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;file&quot;:&quot;Ponce2.ogg&quot;},&quot;classes&quot;:[&quot;ext-phonos-PhonosButton&quot;,&quot;noexcerpt&quot;,&quot;ext-phonos-PhonosButton-emptylabel&quot;]}"><a role="button" tabindex="0" href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/transcoded/f/fb/Ponce2.ogg/Ponce2.ogg.mp3" rel="nofollow" aria-label="Play audio" title="Play audio" class="oo-ui-buttonElement-button"><span class="oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-icon-volumeUp"></span><span class="oo-ui-labelElement-label"></span><span class="oo-ui-indicatorElement-indicator oo-ui-indicatorElement-noIndicator"></span></a></span><sup class="ext-phonos-attribution noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><a href="/wiki/File:Ponce2.ogg" title="File:Ponce2.ogg">\xe2\x93\x98</a></sup></span></span>) is a <a href="/wiki/City" title="City">city</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Municipalities of Puerto Rico">municipality</a> on the southern coast of <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>25<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The most populated city outside the <a href="/wiki/San_Juan,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Juan, Puerto Rico">San Juan</a> metropolitan area, was founded on August 12, 1692<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>note 1<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Salvador_Brau_1820._p._4_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Salvador_Brau_1820._p._4-28"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Jos\xc3\xa9_Leandro_Montalvo-Guenard_1963._p.11_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jos\xc3\xa9_Leandro_Montalvo-Guenard_1963._p.11-21"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Francisco_Lluch_Mora_2006._p._33_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Francisco_Lluch_Mora_2006._p._33-18"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>17<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and is named after <a href="/wiki/Juan_Ponce_de_Le%C3%B3n_y_Loayza" title="Juan Ponce de Le\xc3\xb3n y Loayza">Juan Ponce de Le\xc3\xb3n y Loayza</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> the great-grandson of Spanish conquistador <a href="/wiki/Juan_Ponce_de_Le%C3%B3n" title="Juan Ponce de Le\xc3\xb3n">Juan Ponce de Le\xc3\xb3n</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>note 2<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Ponce is often referred to as <i>La Perla del Sur</i> (The Pearl of the South), <i>La Ciudad Se\xc3\xb1orial</i><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>b<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> (The Manorial City<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>c<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>), and <i>La Ciudad de las Quenepas</i> (<a href="/wiki/Melicoccus_bijugatus" title="Melicoccus bijugatus">Genip</a> City). \n</p><p>The city serves as the governmental seat of the autonomous municipality as well as the regional hub for various <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Government of Puerto Rico">Government of Puerto Rico</a> entities, such as the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Supreme Court of Puerto Rico">Judiciary of Puerto Rico</a>. It is also the regional center for various <a href="/wiki/Federal_government_of_the_United_States" title="Federal government of the United States">U.S. Federal Government</a> agencies. Ponce is a principal city of both the <a href="/wiki/Ponce_metropolitan_area" title="Ponce metropolitan area">Ponce Metropolitan Statistical Area</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Ponce_metropolitan_area#Combined_Statistical_Area" title="Ponce metropolitan area">Ponce-Yauco-Coamo Combined Statistical Area</a>.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Municipalities of Puerto Rico">municipality of Ponce</a>, officially the <i>Autonomous Municipality of Ponce</i>, is located in the southern coastal plain region of the island, south of <a href="/wiki/Adjuntas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Adjuntas, Puerto Rico">Adjuntas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Utuado,_Puerto_Rico" title="Utuado, Puerto Rico">Utuado</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jayuya,_Puerto_Rico" title="Jayuya, Puerto Rico">Jayuya</a>; east of <a href="/wiki/Pe%C3%B1uelas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Pe\xc3\xb1uelas, Puerto Rico">Pe\xc3\xb1uelas</a>; west of <a href="/wiki/Juana_D%C3%ADaz,_Puerto_Rico" title="Juana D\xc3\xadaz, Puerto Rico">Juana D\xc3\xadaz</a>; and bordered on the south by the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">Caribbean Sea</a>. The municipality has 31 <a href="/wiki/Barrio" title="Barrio">barrios</a>, including 19 outside the city\'s urban area and 12 in the urban area of the city. It is the second largest in Puerto Rico by land area, and it was the first in Puerto Rico to obtain its <a href="/wiki/Self-governance" title="Self-governance">autonomy</a>, becoming the <i>Autonomous Municipality of Ponce</i> in 1992.\n</p><p>The historic <i><a href="/wiki/Ponce_Historic_Zone" title="Ponce Historic Zone">Ponce Pueblo</a></i> district, located in the downtown area of the city, is composed by several of the <a href="/wiki/Pueblos_in_Puerto_Rico" title="Pueblos in Puerto Rico">downtown barrios</a>, and is located approximately three miles (4.8&#160;km) inland from the Caribbean coast. The historic district is characterized for its <i><a href="/wiki/Neocl%C3%A1sico_Isabelino" title="Neocl\xc3\xa1sico Isabelino">Neocl\xc3\xa1sico Isabelino</a></i> and <a href="/wiki/Ponce_Creole" title="Ponce Creole">Ponce Creole architectures</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-americanheritage.com_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-americanheritage.com-34"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="History">History</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ponce,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Antigua_Plaza_Real_(luego_llamada_Plaza_Mayor,_y_ahora_Plaza_Degetau),_en_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico,_mirando_al_sureste_desde_la_Calle_Uni%C3%B3n.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img
