colspan="14" style="text-align:center;font-size:95%;">Source: <a href="/wiki/NOAA" class="mw-redirect" title="NOAA">NOAA</a><sup id="cite_ref-NOAA_155-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NOAA-155"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>150<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-NCEI_156-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NCEI-156"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>151<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n</div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Cityscape">Cityscape</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ponce,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Cityscape"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Architecture">Architecture</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ponce,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Architecture"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Weichert-Villaronga.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Weichert-Villaronga.jpg/200px-Weichert-Villaronga.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Weichert-Villaronga.jpg/300px-Weichert-Villaronga.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Weichert-Villaronga.jpg/400px-Weichert-Villaronga.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1200" /></a><figcaption>The <a href="/wiki/Villaronga_Residence" class="mw-redirect" title="Villaronga Residence">Museum of Puerto Rican Architecture</a>, the only architecture museum in the Island, is housed in this 100-year-old residence on Reina Street</figcaption></figure>\n<p>During the 19th century, the city was witness to a flourishing architectural development, including the birth of a new architectural style later dubbed <a href="/wiki/Ponce_Creole" title="Ponce Creole">Ponce Creole</a>. Architects like Francisco Valls, <a href="/wiki/Manuel_V._Domenech" title="Manuel V. Domenech">Manuel V\xc3\xadctor Domenech</a>, Eduardo Salich, <a href="/wiki/Blas_Silva" class="mw-redirect" title="Blas Silva">Blas Silva Boucher</a>, Agust\xc3\xadn Camilo Gonz\xc3\xa1lez, Alfredo Wiechers, <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Porrata_Doria" class="mw-redirect" title="Francisco Porrata Doria">Francisco Porrata Doria</a> and Francisco Gard\xc3\xb3n Vega used a mixture of <a href="/wiki/Art_Nouveau" title="Art Nouveau">Art Nouveau</a> and <a href="/wiki/Neoclassical_architecture" title="Neoclassical architecture">neoclassic</a> styles to give the city a unique look. This can be seen in the various structures located in the center of the city like the <a href="/wiki/Teatro_La_Perla" title="Teatro La Perla">Teatro La Perla</a>. To showcase its rich architectural heritage, the city has opened the <a href="/wiki/Casa_Wiechers-Villaronga" title="Casa Wiechers-Villaronga">Museum of Puerto Rican Architecture</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Casa_Wiechers-Villaronga" title="Casa Wiechers-Villaronga">Wiechers-Villaronga</a> residence.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>152<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>153<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Many of the city\'s features (from house fa\xc3\xa7ades to <a href="/wiki/Chamfer" title="Chamfer">chamfered</a> street corners) are modeled on <a href="/wiki/Barcelona" title="Barcelona">Barcelona</a>\'s architecture, given the city\'s strong <a href="/wiki/Catalan_people" class="mw-redirect" title="Catalan people">Catalan</a> heritage. In 2020, the <a href="/wiki/National_Trust_for_Historic_Preservation" title="National Trust for Historic Preservation">National Trust for Historic Preservation</a> named the Ponce Historic Zone as one of America\'s most endangered historic places.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>154<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Barrios">Barrios</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ponce,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Barrios"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_barrios_of_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="List of barrios of Ponce, Puerto Rico">List of barrios of Ponce, Puerto Rico</a></div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Ponce_barrios_map_labeled.svg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Ponce_barrios_map_labeled.svg/400px-Ponce_barrios_map_labeled.svg.png" decoding="async" width="400" height="400" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Ponce_barrios_map_labeled.svg/600px-Ponce_barrios_map_labeled.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Ponce_barrios_map_labeled.svg/800px-Ponce_barrios_map_labeled.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="765" data-file-height="765" /></a><figcaption></figcaption></figure>\n<p>With 31 <i>barrios</i>, Ponce is Puerto Rico\'s municipality with the largest number of barrios.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>155<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>156<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>157<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>158<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Ponce\'s barrios consist of 12 located in the urban area of the city plus 19 outside the urban zone.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>159<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>160<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Of these nineteen, seven were considered <a href="/wiki/Suburban" class="mw-redirect" title="Suburban">suburban</a> in 1999. The suburban barrios were: <a href="/wiki/Canas_(Ponce)" class="mw-redirect" title="Canas (Ponce)">Canas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magueyes" class="mw-redirect" title="Magueyes">Magueyes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portugu%C3%A9s_Rural" class="mw-redirect" title="Portugu\xc3\xa9s Rural">Portugu\xc3\xa9s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Machuelo_Arriba" title="Machuelo Arriba">Machuelo Arriba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sabanetas_(Ponce)" class="mw-redirect" title="Sabanetas (Ponce)">Sabanetas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coto_Laurel" title="Coto Laurel">Coto Laurel</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cerrillos_(Ponce)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cerrillos (Ponce)">Cerrillos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>161<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> A 2000 report by the U.S. Census Bureau provides detailed demographics statistics for each of Ponce\'s barrios.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>162<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>The 2000 Census showed that Montes Llanos is the least populated barrio in the municipality. Thanks to its larger area, barrio Canas was by far the most populated ward of the municipality.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>163<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> At 68 persons per square mile, <a href="/wiki/San_Patricio_(Ponce)" class="mw-redirect" title="San Patricio (Ponce)">San Patricio</a> was the least populated, while <a href="/wiki/Cuarto_(Ponce)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cuarto (Ponce)">Cuarto</a> was the most densely populated at 18,819 persons per square mile.\n</p><p>Ponce has nine barrios that border neighboring municipalities. These are <a href="/wiki/Canas,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Canas, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Canas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quebrada_Lim%C3%B3n" title="Quebrada Lim\xc3\xb3n">Quebrada Lim\xc3\xb3n</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marue%C3%B1o" title="Marue\xc3\xb1o">Marue\xc3\xb1o</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guaraguao" title="Guaraguao">Guaraguao</a>, <a href="/wiki/San_Patricio,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Patricio, Ponce, Puerto Rico">San Patricio</a>, <a href="/wiki/An%C3%B3n" title="An\xc3\xb3n">An\xc3\xb3n</a>, <a href="/wiki/Real,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Real, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Real</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coto_Laurel" title="Coto Laurel">Coto Laurel</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Capitanejo,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Capitanejo, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Capitanejo</a>. Canas and Capitanejo are also coastal barrios, and together with three others (<a href="/wiki/Playa,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Playa, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Playa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bucan%C3%A1" class="mw-redirect" title="Bucan\xc3\xa1">Bucan\xc3\xa1</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Vayas" class="mw-redirect" title="Vayas">Vayas</a>) make up the municipality\'s five coastal barrios.\n</p><p>There are also five barrios within the city limits (<a href="/wiki/Canas_Urbano" title="Canas Urbano">Canas Urbano</a>, <a href="/wiki/Machuelo_Abajo" title="Machuelo Abajo">Machuelo Abajo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magueyes_Urbano" title="Magueyes Urbano">Magueyes Urbano</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portugu%C3%A9s_Urbano" title="Portugu\xc3\xa9s Urbano">Portugu\xc3\xa9s Urbano</a>, and <a href="/wiki/San_Ant%C3%B3n" title="San Ant\xc3\xb3n">San Ant\xc3\xb3n</a>) that in addition to the original six city core barrios \xe2\x80\x94 named <a href="/wiki/Primero,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Primero, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Primero</a>, <a href="/wiki/Segundo,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Segundo, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Segundo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tercero,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Tercero, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Tercero</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuarto,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Cuarto, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Cuarto</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quinto,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Quinto, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Quinto</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Sexto,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Sexto, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Sexto</a> \xe2\x80\x94 make up the 11 urban zone barrios of the municipality. The <a href="/wiki/Ponce_Historic_Zone" title="Ponce Historic Zone">historic zone</a> of the city is within these original six core city barrios. These eleven barrios composed what is known as the urban zone of the municipality.\n</p><p>The remaining eight barrios (<a href="/wiki/Magueyes" class="mw-redirect" title="Magueyes">Magueyes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tibes" title="Tibes">Tibes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Montes_Llanos" title="Montes Llanos">Montes Llanos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marag%C3%BCez" title="Marag\xc3\xbcez">Marag\xc3\xbcez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portugu%C3%A9s_Rural" class="mw-redirect" title="Portugu\xc3\xa9s Rural">Portugu\xc3\xa9s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Machuelo_Arriba" title="Machuelo Arriba">Machuelo Arriba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cerrillos,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Cerrillos, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Cerrillos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sabanetas,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Sabanetas, Ponce, Puerto Rico">Sabanetas</a>) are located in the interior of the municipality. These last eight are outside the city limits and are neither coastal nor bordering barrios.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>164<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>A summary of all the barrios of the municipality, their population, population density, and land and water areas as given by the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Census_Bureau" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Census Bureau">U.S. Census Bureau</a> is as follows:<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>165<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>166<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>167<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th>No.</th>\n<th>Barrio</th>\n<th>Population<br />(<a href="/wiki/United_States_Census_2000" align="right">78.9\n</td></tr>\n</tbody></table>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Tourism">Tourism</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ponce,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Tourism"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Castillo_Serralles.JPG" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Castillo_Serralles.JPG/200px-Castillo_Serralles.JPG" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Castillo_Serralles.JPG/300px-Castillo_Serralles.JPG 1.5x, href="/wiki/Museo_Castillo_Serrall%C3%A9s" title="Museo Castillo Serrall\xc3\xa9s">Museo Castillo Serrall\xc3\xa9s</a> receives 100,000 visitors a year</figcaption></figure>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Crucero_%27Serenade_of_the_Seas%27_anclando_en_el_Puerto_de_Ponce,_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico,_mirando_al_sureste_(DSC03103).jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Crucero_%27Serenade_of_the_Seas%27_anclando_en_el_Puerto_de_Ponce%2C_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_mirando_al_sureste_%28DSC03103%29.jpg/300px-Crucero_%27Serenade_of_the_Seas%27_anclando_en_el_Puerto_de_Ponce%2C_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_mirando_al_sureste_%28DSC03103%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Crucero_%27Serenade_of_the_Seas%27_anclando_en_el_Puerto_de_Ponce%2C_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_mirando_al_sureste_%28DSC03103%29.jpg/400px-Crucero_%27Serenade_of_the_Seas%27_anclando_en_el_Puerto_de_Ponce%2C_Ponce%2C_Puerto_Rico%2C_mirando_al_sureste_%28DSC03103%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4896" data-file-height="3672" /></a><figcaption>The cruise ship <a href="/wiki/Serenade_of_the_Seas" title="Serenade of the Seas">Serenade of the Seas</a> arriving at the <a href="/wiki/Port_of_Ponce" class="mw-redirect" title="Port of Ponce">Port of Ponce</a> during dawn in early 2020</figcaption></figure>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_tourist_attractions_in_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="List of tourist attractions in Ponce, Puerto Rico">List of tourist attractions in Ponce, Puerto Rico</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nightlife_in_Ponce,_Puerto_Rico" title="Nightlife in Ponce, Puerto Rico">Nightlife in Ponce, Puerto Rico</a></div>\n<p>Due to its historical importance throughout the years, Ponce features many points of interest for visiting tourists.<sup id="cite_ref-JetBlue_2010_173-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JetBlue_2010-173"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>168<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The downtown area contains the bulk of Ponce\'s tourist attractions.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>169<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Tourism has seen significant growth in recent years. In 2007, over 6,000 tourists visited the city via cruise ships.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>170<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Passenger movement at the <a href="/wiki/Mercedita_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Mercedita Airport">Mercedita Airport</a> in <a href="/wiki/Fiscal_year" title="Fiscal year">FY</a> 2008 was 278,911, a 1,228% increase over fiscal year 2003 and the highest of all the regional airports for that 5-year period.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>171<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Though not all of these were tourists, it represents a volume larger than the population of the city itself.\n</p><p>To support a growing tourist industry, around the 1970s, and starting with the Ponce <a href="/wiki/Holiday_Inn" title="Holiday Inn">Holiday Inn</a>, several hotels have been built. Newer lodging additions include the Ponce <a href="/wiki/Hilton_Hotels" class="mw-redirect" title="Hilton Hotels">Hilton</a> Golf &amp; Casino Resort, home to the new Costa Caribe Golf &amp; Country Club, featuring a 27-hole <a href="/wiki/Professional_Golfers%27_Association_of_America" title="Professional Golfers&#39; Association of America">PGA</a> championship <a href="/wiki/Golf_course" title="Golf course">golf course</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Hotel_Meli%C3%A1" title="Hotel Meli\xc3\xa1">Hotel Meli\xc3\xa1</a> has operated in the city continuously since the early 20th century. It has also been studied that the <a href="/wiki/Intercontinental_Hotel,_Ponce" class="mw-redirect" title="Intercontinental Hotel, Ponce">Intercontinental Hotel</a>, which opened in February 1960 and closed in 1975, could be refurbished and re-opened atop the hill near <a href="/wiki/Cruceta_del_Vig%C3%ADa" title="Cruceta del Vig\xc3\xada">Cruceta del Vig\xc3\xada</a> as the "Magna Vista Resort".<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>172<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Ponce_Plaza_Hotel_%26_Casino" title="Ponce Plaza Hotel &amp; Casino">Ponce Ramada</a> also opened in 2009, and other hotel projects in the works include the Four Points by <a href="/wiki/Sheraton_Hotels_and_Resorts" title="Sheraton Hotels and Resorts">Sheraton</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Marriott_International" title="Marriott International">Marriott</a> Courtyard, among others.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>173<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2013, the downtown Ponce Ramada Hotel added a casino to its 70-room structure.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>174<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>175<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Ponce is part of the Government of Puerto Rico\'s <a href="/wiki/Porta_Caribe" title="Porta Caribe">Porta Caribe</a> tourist region.\n</p>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1237879389"><table class="infobox" style="clear: left; float:left;margin:0 1.5em 1.5em 0;"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" class="infobox-above" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Nuvola_apps_arts.svg/16px-Nuvola_apps_arts.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" class="mw-file-element"
